<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the switch package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> zagSwitch</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/switch&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The switch package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:switch/usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div data-scope="tabs" <h3 id="making-it-checked-by-default" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Making it checked by default<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#making-it-checked-by-default"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultChecked</code> property to make a switch checked by default.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>zagSwitch<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultChecked</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-checked-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled checked state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-checked-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">checked</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onCheckedChange</code> for controlled usage.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>zagSwitch<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  checked<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onCheckedChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setChecked</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">checked</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the switch value changes, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onCheckedChange</code> callback is invoked.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>zagSwitch<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onCheckedChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { checked: boolean }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;switch is:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">checked</span> <span class="token operator">?</span> <span class="token string">&quot;On&quot;</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Off&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="programmatic-toggle" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Programmatic toggle<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#programmatic-toggle"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the connected API when you need imperative control.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">setChecked</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<h3 id="usage-within-forms" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Usage within forms<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage-within-forms"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To use switch in forms, set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code> and render <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getHiddenInputProps()</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>zagSwitch<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;feature&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="custom-form-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Custom form value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#custom-form-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> to customize the submitted form value when checked.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>zagSwitch<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;notifications&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">value</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;enabled&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each switch part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="focused-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Focused State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#focused-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the switch input is focused, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-focus</code> attribute is added to the
root, control and label parts.</p>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="disabled-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabled State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabled-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the switch is disabled, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code> attribute is added to the root,

<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The switch machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; hiddenInput: string; control: string; label: string; thumb: string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the switch. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">label</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">Specifies the localized strings that identifies the accessibility elements and their states</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the switch is disabled.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">invalid</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">If `true`, the switch is marked as invalid.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">required</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">If `true`, the switch input is marked as required,</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">readOnly</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the switch is read-only</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onCheckedChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: CheckedChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to call when the switch is clicked.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">checked</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The controlled checked state of the switch</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultChecked</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The initial checked state of the switch when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the checked state of the switch.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The name of the input field in a switch
(Useful for form submission).</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">form</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The id of the form that the switch belongs to</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string | number</code><span class="d_block">The value of switch input. Useful for form submission.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; ShadowRoot | Node | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The switch <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">checked</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the switch is checked</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the switch is disabled</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">focused</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the switch is focused</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setChecked</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(checked: boolean) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Sets the checked state of the switch.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toggleChecked</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Toggles the checked state of the switch.</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="data-attributes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Data Attributes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#data-attributes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Root</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column <h2 id="accessibility" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Accessibility<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Adheres to the
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/switch/" class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px">Switch WAI-ARIA design pattern</a></p>

off.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/switch\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"Switch\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Sync with `disabled` state of fieldset\n- Sync with form `reset` events\n- Can be toggled programmatically\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the switch package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"switch/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the switch anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"switch\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the switch package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as zagSwitch from \"@zag-js/switch\"\n```\n\nThe switch package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"switch/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Making it checked by default\n\nUse the `defaultChecked` property to make a switch checked by default.\n\n```jsx {3}\nconst service = useMachine(zagSwitch.machine, {\n  defaultChecked: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled checked state\n\nUse `checked` and `onCheckedChange` for controlled usage.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(zagSwitch.machine, {\n  checked,\n  onCheckedChange(details) {\n    setChecked(details.checked)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for changes\n\nWhen the switch value changes, the `onCheckedChange` callback is invoked.\n\n```jsx {3-5}\nconst service = useMachine(zagSwitch.machine, {\n  onCheckedChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { checked: boolean }\n    console.log(\"switch is:\", details.checked ? \"On\" : \"Off\")\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Programmatic toggle\n\nUse the connected API when you need imperative control.\n\n```jsx\napi.setChecked(true)\napi.toggleChecked()\n```\n\n### Usage within forms\n\nTo use switch in forms, set `name` and render `api.getHiddenInputProps()`.\n\n```jsx {3}\nconst service = useMachine(zagSwitch.machine, {\n  name: \"feature\",\n})\n```\n\n### Custom form value\n\nSet `value` to customize the submitted form value when checked.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(zagSwitch.machine, {\n  name: \"notifications\",\n  value: \"enabled\",\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach switch part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Focused State\n\nWhen the switch input is focused, the `data-focus` attribute is added to the\nroot, control and label parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for root focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"control\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for control focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for label focus state */\n}\n```\n\n### Disabled State\n\nWhen the switch is disabled, the `data-disabled` attribute is added to the root,\ncontrol and label parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for root disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"control\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for control disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for label disabled state */\n}\n```\n\n### Invalid State\n\nWhen the switch is invalid, the `data-invalid` attribute is added to the root,\ncontrol and label parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for root invalid state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"control\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for control invalid state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for label invalid state */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe switch machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"switch\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe switch `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"switch\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"switch\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\nAdheres to the\n[Switch WAI-ARIA design pattern](https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/switch/)\n\n### Keyboard Interactions\n\n\u003cKeyboardTable name=\"switch\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Switch\",\"description\":\"Using the switch machine in your
